let me start by saying , let's look back to the 20th century , and kind of get a sense of how that style of security worked for us .	讓我先說 , 讓我們回到二十世紀 , 有點像是了解安全風格對我們來說是如何運作的 。
this is verdun , a battlefield in france just north of the nato headquarters in belgium .	這是verdun , 法國北部的一個戰場位於比利時總部的北部 。
at verdun , in 1916 , over a 300day period , 700 , 000 people were killed , so about 2 , 000 a day .	在1916年的verdun , 超過300天的時間 , 70萬人被殺害 , 所以大約每天2 , 000人死亡 。
if you roll it forward 20thcentury security into the second world war , you see the battle of stalingrad , 300 days , 2 million people killed .	如果你把它向前推進20世紀的安全性進入第二次世界大戰 , 你可以看到史達林畢業的戰役 , 300天 , 2百萬人喪命 。
we go into the cold war , and we continue to try and build walls .	我們進入冷戰 , 繼續嘗試建造牆壁 。
we go from the trench warfare of the first world war to the maginot line of the second world war , and then we go into the cold war , the iron curtain , the berlin wall .	我們從第一次世界大戰的示威戰 , 到第二次世界大戰的馬吉尼線 , 然後進入冷戰、鐵幕、柏林圍牆 。
my thesis for us today is , instead of building walls to create security , we need to build bridges .	我今天對我們提出的論點是 , 與其建造牆來創造安全 , 我們需要建造橋樑 。
this is a famous bridge in europe .	這是歐洲一座著名的橋 。
it's the bridge over the drina river , the subject of a novel by ivo andrić , and it talks about how , in that very troubled part of europe and the balkans , over time there's been enormous building of walls .	它是愛因納河的橋樑 , 艾佛•安德里的小說主題 , 它談到 , 在歐洲和巴爾幹半部 , 隨著時間過去 , 已經有了巨大的建物 。
more recently , in the last decade , we begin to see these communities start , hesitatingly , to come together .	更近期 , 在過去十年間 , 我們開始看到這些社區開始 , 猶豫著 , 要團結在一起 。
i would argue , again , opensource security is about connecting the international , the interagency , the privatepublic , and lashing it together with strategic communication , largely in social networks .	我會再說一次 , 開放式安全是把國際、介入、私人共和國連結起來 , 和策略性溝通 , 很大程度上 , 在社群網絡中 。
so let me talk a little bit about why we need to do that , because our global commons is under attack in a variety of ways , and none of the sources of threat to the global commons will be solved by building walls .	所以 , 讓我來談談為什麼我們需要這麼做 , 因為我們的全球公有物正以各種方式受到攻擊 , 沒有任何對全球公有物造成威脅的來源 , 會透過建立牆壁來解決 。
now , i'm a sailor , obviously .	顯然 , 我是個水手 。
this is a ship , a liner , clipping through the indian ocean .	這是一艘船 , 一路線 , 穿越印度洋 。
what's wrong with this picture ?	這張照片有什麼問題 ?
it's got concertina wire along the sides of it .	沿著旁邊的音樂會電線
that's to prevent pirates from attacking it .	也就是防止海盜攻擊它 。
piracy is a very active threat today around the world . this is in the indian ocean .	海盜是全世界非常活躍的威脅 。 這是在印度洋 。
piracy is also very active in the strait of malacca .	海盜也非常活躍在馬拉卡的海峽
it's active in the gulf of guinea .	活躍於幾內亞灣
we see it in the caribbean .	我們在加勒比海看到
it's a $10billionayear discontinuity in the global transport system .	在全球運輸系統中 , 它是十億美元的不連續性 。
last year , at this time , there were 20 vessels , 500 mariners held hostage .	去年 , 在這個時候 , 有20艘船 , 500名馬林人舉辦了人質 。
this is an attack on the global commons .	這是對全球公有物的攻擊 。
we need to think about how to address it .	我們需要考慮如何處理
let's shift to a different kind of sea , the cyber sea .	讓我們轉移到另一種海域 , 網路海域 。
here are photographs of two young men .	這是兩位年輕男子的照片 。
at the moment , they're incarcerated .	在當下 , 他們被監禁 。
they conducted a credit card fraud that netted them over 10 billion dollars .	他們指揮了一個信用卡詐欺案 , 將他們網絡超過一百億美元 。
this is part of cybercrime which is a $2trillionayear discontinuity in the global economy .	這是網路犯罪的一部分這是全球經濟2兆美元的連續性
two trillion a year .	一年有兩兆
that's just under the gdp of great britain .	那只是在英國的國內生產毛額下
so this cyber sea , which we know endlessly is the fundamental piece of radical openness , is very much under threat as well .	這種網路海 , 我們無止境地知道 , 就是極端開放的基本要素 , 也非常受到威脅 。
another thing i worry about in the global commons is the threat posed by trafficking , by the movement of narcotics , opium , here coming out of afghanistan through europe over to the united states .	在全球公有物中 , 我擔心的另一件事 , 是人口販賣所造成的威脅 , 毒品、鴉片 , 在這裡 , 從阿富汗來到美國 。
we worry about cocaine coming from the andean ridge north .	我們擔心從安地斯山北邊來的古柯鹼 。
we worry about the movement of illegal weapons and trafficking . above all , perhaps , we worry about human trafficking , and the awful cost of it .	我們擔心非法武器和販賣 。 最重要的是 , 我們擔心人口販賣 , 以及它的代價 。
trafficking moves largely at sea but in other parts of the global commons .	人口販賣大量地在海上移動 , 但在全球公有物的其他地方 。
this is a photograph , and i wish i could tell you that this is a very hightech piece of us navy gear that we're using to stop the trafficking .	這是一張照片 , 我真希望我能告訴你這是我們海軍海軍的一個高科技小貨幣我們用來阻止人口販賣 。
the bad news is , this is a semisubmersible run by drug cartels .	壞消息是 , 這是毒品卡特爾的半開銷 。
it was built in the jungles of south america .	在南美叢林中被建造出來 。
we caught it with that lowtech raft — — and it was carrying six tons of cocaine .	我們用那低科技的木筏抓到它 , 它帶著六噸的古柯鹼 。
crew of four . sophisticated communications sweep .	四個組員 。 精密的溝通打掃了 。
this kind of trafficking , in narcotics , in humans , in weapons , god forbid , in weapons of mass destruction , is part of the threat to the global commons .	這種販賣 , 在毒品中 , 在人中 , 在武器中 , 上帝禁止 , 在大規模破壞的武器中 , 是對全球公有物造成威脅的一部分 。
and let's pull it together in afghanistan today .	今天讓我們一起在阿富汗
this is a field of poppies in afghanistan .	這是阿富汗的一塊大便領域 。
eighty to 90 percent of the world's poppy , opium and heroin , comes out of afghanistan .	世界上百分之八十到九十的大豆、鴉片和海洛因 , 都從阿富汗出來 。
we also see there , of course , terrorism .	當然 , 我們也在那裡看到恐怖主義 。
this is where al qaeda is staged from .	這是基地組織所在的地方 。
we also see a very strong insurgency embedded there .	我們也看到一個非常強烈的暴動發生在那裏 。
so this terrorism concern is also part of the global commons , and what we must address .	所以 , 這種恐怖主義的擔憂也是全球公有物的一部分 , 我們必須要處理的 。
so here we are , 21st century .	現在 , 21世紀 ,
we know our 20thcentury tools are not going to work .	我們知道我們的20世紀工具是行不通的
what should we do ?	我們應該怎麼做 ?
i would argue that we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我主張我們不能只靠一把槍支來遞送安全 。
we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我們不能只靠槍支來遞送安全 。
we will need the application of military force .	我們將需要軍事力量的應用 。
when we do it , we must do it well , and competently .	當我們這樣做時 , 我們一定要做得很好 , 且要有競爭力 。
but my thesis is , opensource security is about international , interagency , privatepublic connection pulled together by this idea of strategic communication on the internet .	但我的論點是 , 開放原始碼的安全是關於國際、介入、私人公共的連結 , 透過網路上策略性溝通的概念來結合在一起 。
let me give you a couple of examples of how this works in a positive way .	讓我用正面的方式來舉幾個例子 。
this is afghanistan . these are afghan soldiers .	這是阿富汗 , 這些是阿富汗士兵
they are all holding books .	他們都拿著書 。
you should say , " that's odd . i thought i read that this demographic , young men and women in their 20s and 30s , is largely illiterate in afghanistan . "	你應該說: 「 這很奇怪 。 我想我讀到 , 這種人口統計 , 年輕男女在20、30多歲時 , 很大程度上是阿富汗的文盲 。 」
you would be correct .	你會是正確的 。
eightyfive percent cannot read when they enter the security forces of afghanistan .	當他們進入阿富汗的安全部隊時 , 85%無法閱讀 。
why ? because the taliban withheld education during the period of time in which these men and women would have learned to read .	為甚麼呢 ? 因為塔利班在那段時間內接受良好教育 , 這些男女會學會閱讀 。
so the question is , so , why are they all standing there holding books ?	所以問題是 , 為什麼他們都站在那裡拿著書 ?
the answer is , we are teaching them to read in literacy courses by nato in partnership with private sector entities , in partnership with development agencies .	答案是 , 我們在教導他們在讀讀讀讀讀寫能力的課程 , 由北約組織和私人機構合作 , 和開發機構合作 。
we've taught well over 200 , 000 afghan security forces to read and write at a basic level .	我們教會了超過二十萬名阿富汗安全部隊 , 以基本的水平閱讀和寫 。
when you can read and write in afghanistan , you will typically put a pen in your pocket .	當你能在阿富汗讀和寫時 , 你通常會在你的口袋裡放一支筆 。
at the ceremonies , when these young men and women graduate , they take that pen with great pride , and put it in their pocket .	在典禮上 , 當這些年輕男女畢業時 , 他們用很棒的驕傲 , 把它放在他們的口袋裡 。
this is bringing together international — there are 50 nations involved in this mission — interagency — these development agencies — and privatepublic , to take on this kind of security .	這讓國際組織起來--有50個國家參與這項任務--介入這些發展機構和私人共和國 , 來採取這種安全措施 。
now , we are also teaching them combat skills , of course , but i would argue , opensource security means connecting in ways that create longer lasting security effect .	當然 , 我們也在教導他們戰鬥技巧 , 但我認為 , 開放原始碼的安全意味著用能創造更長久的安全效果的方式來連結 。
this is a us navy warship .	這是美國海軍戰艦 。
it's called the comfort .	叫做舒適感 。
there's a sister ship called the mercy .	有一艘名叫mercy的姐妹船
they are hospital ships .	他們是醫院的船隻 。
this one , the comfort , operates throughout the caribbean and the coast of south america conducting patient treatments .	這個 , 安慰劑在加勒比海和南美洲的海岸進行病人的治療 。
on a typical cruise , they'll do 400 , 000 patient treatments .	在典型的途中 , 他們會做四十萬個病人的治療 。
it is crewed not strictly by military but by a combination of humanitarian organizations: operation hope , project smile .	它不被軍隊認可 , 而是結合了人道主義組織:願望 , 微笑 。
other organizations send volunteers .	其他組織發送志工
interagency physicians come out .	介入醫師出來
they're all part of this .	他們都是這方面的一部分 。
to give you one example of the impact this can have , this little boy , eight years old , walked with his mother two days to come to the eye clinic put on by the comfort .	舉個例子 , 這位小男孩 , 八歲 , 和他的媽媽走了兩天 , 來到舒適的眼科診所 。
when he was fitted , over his extremely myopic eyes , he suddenly looked up and said , " mama , veo el mundo . "	當他被配合時 , 在他極度神秘的眼神之中 , 他突然抬頭說: 「 媽媽 , veoelmundo 。 」
" mom , i see the world . "	「 媽媽 , 我看到這個世界 。 」
multiply this by 400 , 000 patient treatments , this privatepublic collaboration with security forces , and you begin to see the power of creating security in a very different way .	乘以四十萬個病人的治療 , 這種私人和安全部隊合作 , 你開始看到創造安全的力量 , 以非常不同的方式創造安全 。
here you see baseball players .	這裡你看到棒球員
can you pick out the two us army soldiers in this photograph ?	你能在這張照片中挑出兩名美國軍人嗎 ?
they are the two young men on either side of these young boys . this is part of a series of baseball clinics , where we have explored collaboration between major league baseball , the department of state , who sets up the diplomatic piece of this , military baseball players , who are real soldiers with real skills but participate in this mission , and they put on clinics throughout latin america and the caribbean , in honduras , in nicaragua , in all of the central american and caribbean nations where baseball is so popular , and it creates security .	他們是這兩位年輕男孩兩邊的年輕人 。 這是一系列棒球診所的一部分 , 我們在拉丁美洲和加勒比海的大聯盟合作 , 國務院 , 設立了外交部 , 軍事棒球選手 , 他們是真正的軍人 , 但參與了這個任務 , 他們在整個拉丁美洲和加勒比海 , 尼加拉瓜和加拉瓜 , 全美各地都是棒球棒球聯盟 。
it shows role models to young men and women about fitness and about life that i would argue help create security for us .	它展示給年輕男女關於健身及人生的榜樣 , 我主張要為我們創造安全 。
another aspect of this partnership is in disaster relief .	這個合作關係的另一個面向是在災難救援中 。
this is a us air force helicopter participating after the tsunami in 2004 which killed 250 , 000 people .	這是一架美國空軍直升機在2004年海嘯後參與 , 造成25萬人死亡 。
in each of these major disasters — the tsunami in 2004 , 250 , 000 dead , the kashmiri earthquake in pakistan , 2005 , 85 , 000 dead , the haitian earthquake , about 300 , 000 dead , more recently the awful earthquaketsunami combination which struck japan and its nuclear industry — in all of these instances , we see partnerships between international actors , interagency , privatepublic working with security forces to respond to this kind of natural disaster .	在這些重大災難中 , 2004年的海嘯 , 25萬人死亡 , 巴基斯坦的卡許米里地震 , 2005年 , 8萬5千人死亡 , 海地地震 , 大約有30萬人死亡 , 更近代的是近期的地震海嘯組合 , 使得日本及其核能產業在所有這些國家之間 , 我們看到國際演員之間的合作關係 , 跨部門 , 私人和保安部隊合作 , 與自然災害的合作 。
so these are examples of this idea of opensource security .	這些都是開放式安全概念的例子 。
we tie it together , increasingly , by doing things like this .	我們將它綁在一起 , 漸漸地 , 透過這樣做 。
now , you're looking at this thinking , " ah , admiral , these must be sea lanes of communication , or these might be fiber optic cables . "	現在 , 你看著這個想法: 「 啊 , 阿米羅 , 這些一定是溝通的海道 , 或者這些可能是光纖電纜 。 」
no . this is a graphic of the world according to twitter .	不 , 這是根據推特的圖表
purple are tweets . green are geolocation .	紫色是推特 , 綠色是地理分配 。
white is the synthesis .	白色是綜合體 。
it's a perfect evocation of that great population survey , the six largest nations in the world in descending order: china , india , facebook , the united states , twitter and indonesia .	這是個完美的進化 , 大眾調查 , 世界上最大的六個國家有下降秩序:中國、印度、臉書、美國、推特 , 和印尼 。
why do we want to get in these nets ?	我們為什麼要拿到這些蚊帳 ?
why do we want to be involved ?	我們為什麼想要參與 ?
we talked earlier about the arab spring , and the power of all this .	我們先前談到阿拉伯之春 , 以及這一切的力量 。
i'll give you another example , and it's how you move this message .	我再舉一個例子 , 就是你如何移動這個訊息 。
i gave a talk like this in london a while back about this point . i said , as i say to all of you , i'm on facebook . friend me .	我在倫敦做過這樣的演講 , 前陣子提到這個時點 。 我跟你們所有人說 , 我在臉書上 , 朋友給我 。
got a little laugh from the audience .	從觀眾那裡得到一點笑聲 。
there was an article which was run by ap , on the wire .	當時有一篇文章由ap經營 , 在電線上
got picked up in two places in the world: finland and indonesia .	在世界上兩個地方被撿到:芬蘭和印尼 。
the headline was: nato admiral needs friends .	標題是:娜托•阿德道德需要朋友 。
and the story was a catalyst , and the next morning i had hundreds of facebook friend requests from indonesians and finns , mostly saying , " admiral , we heard you need a friend , and oh , by the way , what is nato ? "	故事是催化劑 , 隔天早上我有數百個facebook好友請求 , 來自印尼人和芬恩人 , 大部分都會說: 「 阿道德 , 我們聽到你需要一個朋友 , 噢 , 順帶一提 , nato是什麼 ? 」
yeah , we laugh , but this is how we move the message , and moving that message is how we connect international , interagency , privatepublic , and these social nets to help create security .	沒錯 , 我們笑了 , 但這是我們移動訊息的方式 , 移動那訊息是我們如何連結國際、介入、私人共和國 , 以及這些社群網絡 , 來協助創造安全 。
now , let me hit a somber note .	現在 , 讓我按一個11月的音
this is a photograph of a brave british soldier .	這是一名勇敢的英國士兵的照片 。
he's in the scots guards .	他在蘇格蘭衛隊
he's standing the watch in helmand , in southern afghanistan .	他正站在helmand , 在阿富汗南部
i put him here to remind us , i would not want anyone to leave the room thinking that we do not need capable , competent militaries who can create real military effect .	我讓他來提醒我們 , 我不想讓任何人離開房間 , 認為我們不需要有能力、有能力的軍隊 , 能夠創造出真正的軍事效應 。
that is the core of who we are and what we do , and we do it to protect freedom , freedom of speech , all the things we treasure in our societies .	那是我們是誰以及我們所做的事的核心 , 我們為了保護自由 , 言論自由 , 所有我們在社會中珍視的東西 。
but , you know , life is not an onandoff switch .	但 , 你知道的 , 生命不是一個大開關 。
you don't have to have a military that is either in hard combat or is in the barracks .	你不需要有軍隊要麼在艱難戰鬥中 , 要麼就在巴拉克 。
i would argue life is a rheostat .	我會主張生命是旋律 。
you have to dial it in , and as i think about how we create security in this 21st century , there will be times when we will apply hard power in true war and crisis , but there will be many instances , as we've talked about today , where our militaries can be part of creating 21stcentury security , international , interagency , privatepublic , connected with competent communication .	你必須將它撥入其中 , 正如我思考我們如何在21世紀創造安全 , 有時候我們將要在真正的戰爭和危機中應用硬實力 , 但有許多的例子 , 如我們今天所談到的 , 我們的軍隊可以成為創造21世紀安全的一員 , 國際、國際、國際、私人、私人連結的一員 。
i would close by saying that we heard earlier today about wikipedia . i use wikipedia all the time to look up facts , and as all of you appreciate , wikipedia is not created by 12 brilliant people locked in a room writing articles .	最後我要說我們今天早些時候聽到維基百科我常用維基百科查看事實正如你們所有人所欣賞的維基百科都不是由12個聰明人鎖定在一個房間裡寫文章
wikipedia , every day , is tens of thousands of people inputting information , and every day millions of people withdrawing that information .	維基百科 , 每天都有成千上萬的人在輸入資訊 , 每一天 , 數百萬人都退縮了這些資訊 。
it's a perfect image for the fundamental point that no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	這是基本的圖像 , 沒有人跟我們一起思考的一樣聰明 。
no one person , no one alliance , no one nation , no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	沒有一個人 , 沒有一個同盟國 , 沒有一個國家 , 沒有一個人和我們一起想的一樣聰明 。
the vision statement of wikipedia is very simple: a world in which every human being can freely share in the sum of all knowledge .	維基的願景很簡單:一個每個人可以自由地分享在所有知識的總和中的世界 。
my thesis for you is that by combining international , interagency , privatepublic , strategic communication , together , in this 21st century , we can create the sum of all security .	我的論點是 , 透過結合國際、介入、私人共和、策略性的溝通 , 同心協力 , 在21世紀 , 我們就能創造出所有安全的總和 。
thank you very much . thank you . thank you .	非常感謝 。 謝謝 。 謝謝 。
